It builds across heavy industrial, civil/marine, water/wastewater, automotive, energy, healthcare, and commercial markets in the U.S., Canada, and Mexico through 13 operating companies and divisions including Alberici Constructors, Flintco, Hillsdale Fabricators, Filanc, CAS Constructors, and WWPS.",
